  <script type="text/javascript">
var _mlCallInitCallback = function(){};

window.handleCallbackOSM = function(callback) {callback();};

(function(){
  var duringLoad = false;
  var delayed = [];
  var loadQueue = [];
  
  var handleDelayed = function() {for (var c = 0; c < delayed.length; c++) handleCallbackOSM(delayed[c]);};
  
  var load = function(args){ // Modernizr.load wrapper
  if (typeof window.yepnope !== "undefined")
  {
    if (loadQueue.length > 0)
    {
      var q = loadQueue;
      loadQueue = [];
      yepnope(q);
    }
    yepnope(args);
  }
  else
    loadQueue.push(args);
  };

  window.loadMapJS = function (callback) {
  if (callback === null && loadQueue.length == 0) return;
  if (typeof L != 'undefined') return handleCallbackOSM(callback);
  if (callback !== null && duringLoad) {delayed.push(callback); return;}
  duringLoad = true;
  load({load: [window.LEAFLET_URL, window.LEAFLET_URL.replace("leaflet", "maplib")],complete: function()
     {
       window.waitMapsID = setInterval(function()
       {
         if (typeof L == 'undefined') return console.log('Leaflet not loaded yet...');
         if (typeof mL_createMap == 'undefined') return console.log('Maplib not loaded yet...');

         clearInterval(window.waitMapsID);

         window.mL_LoadMapJS = loadMapJS;
         if (callback !== null) handleCallbackOSM(callback);
         handleDelayed();
        },25);
     }});
  };

  window.skipAutoloadOSM = true;
  window.mL_LoadMapJS = loadMapJS;
})();

function GradientBarMouseMove() {}
function GradientBarMouseOut() {}
function GradientBarMouseLeave() {}

function loadBoxMap()
{
  yepnope({load: [window.LEAFLET_URL, window.LEAFLET_URL.replace("leaflet", "maplib"), window.LEAFLET_URL.replace("leaflet", "dygraph-mine"), window.LEAFLET_URL.replace("leaflet", "boxMap")],
  complete: function(){window.mL_LoadMapJS = window.loadMapJS;initBoxMapPopupOptions();handleCallbackOSM(window.loadGMAP);}});
}
</script>

function load_msnmap3121415()
{
 if(window.L_invalidinvoketarget_text)
 {
 var map_msn = new VEMap('myMap3121415');
 map_msn.LoadMap();
 var lat = '40.5893';
 var lon = '-98.3917';
 var zoom = '10';
 map_msn.SetCenterAndZoom(new VELatLong(lat, lon), zoom);
 clearInterval(intervalId);
 } else {
 window.status = intervalCount++;
 if(intervalCount>10) clearInterval(intervalId);
 }
}


function load_googlemap3121415()
{
if (typeof google == 'undefined')
 return jQuery.getScript("http://www.google.com/jsapi?key=ABQIAAAAW4xxdiJ_DmGWpVgHRyCMmRSRX7L3kFzbZax_udZcvCoMcbWvqhRKjSG5ql7ZPbPBVpGab3ynclCLDg", load_googlemap3121415);

if (typeof google.maps == 'undefined')
 return google.load('maps', '3', { 'callback': load_googlemap3121415, other_params:'key=AIzaSyBrfouXHg6NeyNujjnphmV3W39EgRS_FkM&sensor=false'});

function getBoundsZoomLevel(bd, mapDim) {
 var WORLD_DIM = { height: 256, width: 256 };
 var ZOOM_MAX = 21;
 function latRad(lat) { var sin = Math.sin(lat * Math.PI / 180); var radX2 = Math.log((1 + sin) / (1 - sin)) / 2; return Math.max(Math.min(radX2, Math.PI), -Math.PI) / 2;}
 function zoom(mapPx, worldPx, fraction) {return Math.floor(Math.log(mapPx / worldPx / fraction) / Math.LN2);}
 var ne = bd.getNorthEast();
 var sw = bd.getSouthWest();
 var latFraction = (latRad(ne.lat()) - latRad(sw.lat())) / Math.PI;
 var lngDiff = ne.lng() - sw.lng();
 var lngFraction = ((lngDiff < 0) ? (lngDiff + 360) : lngDiff) / 360;
 var latZoom = zoom(mapDim.height, WORLD_DIM.height, latFraction);
 var lngZoom = zoom(mapDim.width, WORLD_DIM.width, lngFraction);
 return Math.min(latZoom, lngZoom, ZOOM_MAX);
}

 var gc = document.getElementById('mapbox13121415');
 var zlev = getBoundsZoomLevel(new google.maps.LatLngBounds(new google.maps.LatLng(40.5338,-98.4472),new google.maps.LatLng(40.6448,-98.3362)), {width:parseInt(gc.style.width), height:parseInt(gc.style.height)});
 var mapOptions = {zoom: zlev, center: new google.maps.LatLng(40.5893, -98.3917), mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP};
 var map_google = new google.maps.Map(gc,mapOptions);
}

function load_osmmap3121415()
{
var map_osm = mL_createMap("osmbox3121415");
var zlev = map_osm.getBoundsZoom(new L.LatLngBounds( new L.LatLng(40.5338,-98.4472), new L.LatLng(40.6448,-98.3362)));
map_osm.setView(new L.LatLng(40.5893, -98.3917), zlev);
}

     <script>
function loadBoxMap() 
{
  var U=window.LEAFLET_URL.replace("http:", "https:"), QUEUE = [U, U.replace('leaflet', 'maplib'), U.replace('leaflet.js', 'boxMap.js?v=7.111')];
  
  if (typeof L  != 'undefined') QUEUE.shift(); //already loaded
    
  yepnope({load: QUEUE, complete: function()
  {
    window.waitMapsBmID = setInterval(function()
    {
      if (typeof L == 'undefined') return console.log('Leaflet not loaded yet[bm]...');
      if (typeof mL_createMap == 'undefined') return console.log('Maplib not loaded yet[bm]...');
	  if (typeof loadGMAP == 'undefined') return console.log('boxMAP not loaded yet[bm]...');

	  clearInterval(window.waitMapsBmID);

      window.mL_LoadMapJS = window.loadMapJS;
	  initBoxMapPopupOptions();
	  handleCallbackOSM(window.loadGMAP);
	}, 25);
  }});
}
</script>

function initBoxMapPopupOptions()
{  
if (typeof bAPI == 'undefined')
    window.bAPI = window; // for compatiblity with previous version
  var container = document.getElementById('bMAPpopUPpredefinedPAT');
  if (container !== null)
  {  
  
  }
  if (1 && typeof window.SKIP_OSM_EVENT_SHIELD == 'undefined' && typeof eventShield != 'undefined') 
{
  new eventShield('eventSHIELD', 'boxMAPborder', 1000);
  if (typeof document.getElementsByClassName != 'undefined')
  {
	  var md = document.getElementsByClassName('mapdiv');
	  if (md.length == 1)
	  {
		  md = md[0];
		  md.id = "mapdiv1234";
		  md.style.position = 'relative';
		  new eventShield('eventSHIELD2', md.id, 1000);
	  }
  }
}
}

    <section id="tornados" class="tornados">
     <h3>Tornado activity:</h3> 
     <p style="margin-top:0px;"><b>Hastings-area historical tornado activity is</b> slightly above <b>Nebraska state average. It is</b> 130% <b>greater than the overall U.S. average.</b><br> </p>
     <p><b>On </b>5/5/1964<b>, a </b><b>category </b>F5 (<b>max. wind speeds</b> 261-318 mph) <b>tornado </b>2.9 <b>miles away from the Hastings city center </b><b>killed</b> 4 <b>people</b> <b>and injured</b> 50 <b>people</b> <b>and caused</b> <b>between</b> $500,000 <b>and</b> $5,000,000 <b>in damages.</b></p> 
     <p><b>On </b>5/10/1985<b>, a </b><b>category </b>F4 (<b>max. wind speeds</b> 207-260 mph) <b>tornado </b>16.8 <b>miles away from the city center </b> <b>injured</b> 2 <b>people</b> <b>and caused</b> <b>between</b> $500,000 <b>and</b> $5,000,000 <b>in damages.</b></p> 
     <p></p>
    </section> 
    <section id="earthquakes" class="earthquakes">
     <h3>Earthquake activity:</h3> <b>Hastings-area historical earthquake activity is </b>near<b> Nebraska state average. It is </b>62% smaller <b>than the overall U.S. average.</b>
     <br> 
     <br><b>On </b>8/18/1959 <b>at </b>06:37:13<b>, a magnitude</b> 7.7 (7.7 UK<b>, Class:</b> Major<b>, Intensity:</b> VIII - XII) <b>earthquake occurred</b> 681.6 <b>miles away from the city center, causing</b> $26,000,000 <b>total damage</b>

     <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
var isIE    = (/msie/i.test(navigator.userAgent) && !/opera/i.test(navigator.userAgent));    
var colurl = '/cost-of-living/col.php';
  
var coldefaultstate = 'NE';
var coldefaultcity = 'Hastings';

function colAjaxRequest(reset) {
    var req = false;
    // Opera, Mozilla, etc.
    if(window.XMLHttpRequest){req=new XMLHttpRequest();if(!isIE && req.overrideMimetype){req.overrideMimeType('text/plain');}} 
    //IE
    else if(window.ActiveXObject){try{req=new ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");}catch(e){try{req=new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");} catch(e){}}}    
    
    req.onreadystatechange = function() { if (req.readyState == 4 && ((req.status == 0) || (req.status == 200))) { colHandleRequest(req); } };
    if(reset==true)
    {
        req.open('GET', '/cost-of-living/col.php');
        req.send(null);            
    } else if(colCreateUrl()==true) {
        req.open('GET', colurl);
        req.send(null);    
    } 
}

function colHandleRequest(req) {    
    var ac = document.getElementById('colForm');
    ac.innerHTML = req.responseText;
    
    var originstate = document.getElementById('originstate');
    if(originstate && originstate.value != 'undefined' && originstate.value == '')
    {
        originstate.value = coldefaultstate;
    }    
    var origincity = document.getElementById('origincity');
    if(origincity && origincity.value != 'undefined' && origincity.value == '')
    {
        var coli,coll=origincity.length;
        for(coli=0;coli<coll;coli++){
            if(origincity[coli].text==coldefaultcity)
            {
                origincity.value = origincity[coli].value;
            }    
        }
    }        
}

function colCreateUrl() {
    colurl = '/cost-of-living/col.php';    
    var salary = document.getElementById('salary');
    if(salary)
    {
        colurl = colurl + '?salary=' + salary.value;
        
        var originstate = document.getElementById('originstate');
        var destinationstate = document.getElementById('destinationstate');
        var origincity = document.getElementById('origincity');
        var destinationcity = document.getElementById('destinationcity');
        
        if(originstate.value != 'undefined' && originstate.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&originstate=' + originstate.value; }
        if(destinationstate.value != 'undefined' && destinationstate.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&destinationstate=' + destinationstate.value; }

        if(origincity && origincity.value != 'undefined' && origincity.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&origincity=' + origincity.value; }
        if(destinationcity && destinationcity.value != 'undefined' && destinationcity.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&destinationcity=' + destinationcity.value; }

        if(origincity && destinationcity && origincity.value != 'undefined' && origincity.value != '' && destinationcity.value != 'undefined' && destinationcity.value != '')        
        {
            return true;
        }   

        if(!origincity && !destinationcity && originstate.value != 'undefined' && originstate.value != '' && destinationstate.value != 'undefined' && destinationstate.value != '')        
        {
            return true;
        }    
        
        return false;
    }    
}
</script>

if (!document.getElementsByClassName) {
  document.getElementsByClassName = function(search) {
    var d = document, elements, pattern, i, results = [];
    if (d.querySelectorAll) { // IE8
      return d.querySelectorAll("." + search);
    }
    if (d.evaluate) { // IE6, IE7
      pattern = ".//*[contains(concat(' ', @class, ' '), ' " + search + " ')]";
      elements = d.evaluate(pattern, d, null, 0, null);
      while ((i = elements.iterateNext())) {
        results.push(i);
      }
    } else {
      elements = d.getElementsByTagName("*");
      pattern = new RegExp("(^|\\s)" + search + "(\\s|$)");
      for (i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
        if ( pattern.test(elements[i].className) ) {
          results.push(elements[i]);
        }
      }
    }
    return results;
  }
}

{

}

  <script>
	

function handleScroll()
{  
  var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
  if (window.lastScrollTop === scrollTop) return;  
  window.lastScrollTop = scrollTop;
  
  if (scrollTop > 100)
    $('.scroll-top-wrapper').addClass('show');
  else
    $('.scroll-top-wrapper').removeClass('show');
}
   

function scrollToTop() {
    verticalOffset = typeof(verticalOffset) != 'undefined' ? verticalOffset : 0;
    element = $('body');
    offset = element.offset();
    offsetTop = offset.top;
    $('html, body').animate({scrollTop: offsetTop}, 500, 'linear');
}
   
$(document).ready(function()
{
  $('.scroll-top-wrapper').on('click', scrollToTop);
    
  var waiting = false, endScrollHandle = void 0;  
  $(document).on( 'ready', handleScroll); 
  $(document).scroll(function () 
  {
    if (waiting) return;
    waiting = true;

    // clear previous scheduled endScrollHandle
    clearTimeout(endScrollHandle);

    handleScroll();

    setTimeout(function () {waiting = false;}, 100);

    // schedule an extra execution of scroll() after 200ms in case the scrolling stops in next 100ms
    endScrollHandle = setTimeout(handleScroll, 200);
  });
    
});
 


	</script>

  <script>
var sortableCNT = 0;
window.sortableTables = [];

var TINY = {};
function T$(i) { return document.getElementById(i) }
function T$$(e, p) { return p.getElementsByTagName(e) }

TINY.table = function() {
    function sorter(n) { this.n = n; this.sortD = 0; this.sortC = 0}
    
	sorter.prototype.init = function(e, f, r) {
        var t = ge(e), i = 0; this.e = e; this.l = t.r.length; t.a = [];
        t.h = T$$('thead', T$(e))[0].rows[r]; t.w = t.h.cells.length;
        for (i; i < t.w; i++) {
            var c = t.h.cells[i];
            if (c.className != 'nosort') {
            
				var icon = "<span class='badge alert-info'>" + 
				           "<span class='glyphicon glyphicon-sort-by-attributes-alt' aria-hidden='true'></span>" +
				           "<span class='glyphicon glyphicon-sort-by-attributes' aria-hidden='true'></span>" +
				           "<span class='glyphicon glyphicon-sort' aria-hidden='true'></span>" +
				           "</span>";
            
				//$(c).prepend(icon);
                c.innerHTML = icon + c.innerHTML
                c.className = this.head;
                c.onclick = new Function('window.sortableTables["' + this.n + '"].wk(this.cellIndex)')
            }
        }
        for (i = 0; i < this.l; i++) { t.a[i] = {} }		
        if (f != -1) t.h.cells[f].className = (this.sortD) ? this.desc : this.asc;
    };
    sorter.prototype.wk = function(y) {
        var t = ge(this.e), x = t.h.cells[y], i = 0;
        for (i; i < this.l; i++) {
            t.a[i].o = i; var v = t.r[i].cells[y];
            t.a[i].v = v.textContent || v.innerText;
        }

        t.p = this.sortC;
		    if (y != t.p) t.h.cells[t.p].className = this.head;
                        
        if ((x.className == this.head)) { t.d = 0; t.p = y; x.className = this.asc; t.a.sort(cp); }
		    //$("#" + this.e + " th").removeClass().addClass(this.head);
        if (t.p == y) { t.a.reverse(); x.className = t.d ? this.asc : this.desc; t.d = t.d ? 0 : 1 }
        else { t.p = y; t.a.sort(cp); t.d = 0; x.className = this.asc }

        var n = document.createElement('tbody');
        for (i = 0; i < this.l; i++) {
            var r = t.r[t.a[i].o].cloneNode(true);
            r.className = t.r[t.a[i].o].className;
            n.appendChild(r);
        }
        t.replaceChild(n, t.b);

        this.sortC = y;
        this.sortD = t.d;
    };

    function ge(e) { var t = T$(e); t.b = T$$('tbody', t)[0]; t.r = t.b.rows; return t };
    function cp(f, c) {
        var g, h; f = g = f.v.toLowerCase(), c = h = c.v.toLowerCase();
        var i = parseFloat(f.replace(/(\$|\,|\%|over| \>|\+)/g, '')), n = parseFloat(c.replace(/(\$|\,|\%|over |\>|\+)/g, ''));
        if (!isNaN(i) && !isNaN(n)) { g = i, h = n }
        return g > h ? 1 : (g < h ? -1 : 0)
    };
    return { sorter: sorter }
} ();

var hasClass = function (el, className) {
    return el.classList ? el.classList.contains(className) : new RegExp('\\b'+ className+'\\b').test(el.className);
};

var extendOpts = function(def, cfg) {
   var opts = def;
   if (typeof cfg == 'string') cfg = JSON.parse(cfg);
   for(var key in cfg) if(cfg.hasOwnProperty(key)) opts[key] = cfg[key];   
   return opts;
};

var setupTblSort = function (table, options) {
    var settings = extendOpts({	sortDIR: 0, sortCOL: 0, theadROW: 0, headCLASS: 'head', ascCLASS: 'asc', descCLASS: 'desc'}, options );
    
    var ID = table.id;		
	  if (ID === void 0 || ID === "")
	  {
	    ID = sortableCNT.toString();
		  table.id = ID;
		  sortableCNT++;
	  }
	
	if (window.sortableTables[ID] !== void 0) return;
	
	var dataOpts = table.getAttribute('data-options');
  if (dataOpts != void 0) settings = extendOpts(settings, dataOpts);

		
	var sorter = new TINY.table.sorter(ID);
	window.sortableTables[ID] = sorter;
	sorter.sortD = settings.sortDIR;
	sorter.head  = settings.headCLASS;
	sorter.asc   = settings.ascCLASS;
	sorter.desc  = settings.descCLASS;
	sorter.init(ID, settings.sortCOL, settings.theadROW);
	if (!hasClass(table, 'tblsort')) table.className += " tblsort";
};


window.jQueryQueue.push(function () 
{
  $.fn.sortableTable = function( options ) 
  {	
	  this.filter( "table" ).each(function() { setupTblSort(this, options);});	
	  return this;
  };
  
  window.initTblSort = function(selector, params) {$(selector).sortableTable(params);};  
});       

</script>

$(document).ready(function(){

var eventShieldCNT = 0;
window.eventShieldTAB = [];

function eventShield(shieldedID, ms) {
this.shieldID = "evtShield_" + shieldedID;
this.shieldedID = shieldedID;
this.shieldTimeoutID = null;
this.ms = ms;
this.shieldedDIV = $("#" + this.shieldedID);
this.shieldDIV = $('<div class="eventShield" id="' + this.shieldID + '"></div>');
this.shieldedDIV.css('position', 'relative');
this.shieldedDIV.append(this.shieldDIV);

//this.shieldDIV.css('opacity', '0.3').css('background', 'red');

//back to DOM objects
this.shieldDIV = this.shieldDIV[0];
this.shieldedDIV = this.shieldedDIV[0];

var th = this;
eventShieldTAB[this.shieldID] = this;
this.shieldDIV.onmouseover = function () { th.DeactivStart(); };
this.shieldDIV.onmouseout = function () { th.DeactivEnd(); };
this.shieldDIV.onclick = function (e) { th.MouseClick(e); };
this.shieldDIV.onmousemove = function () { th.MouseMove(); };
$(document).on( 'scroll', function(){eventShieldTAB[th.shieldID].IsVisible();});
}
        
eventShield.dispatchEvent = function (el, evt) { if (el.dispatchEvent) el.dispatchEvent(evt); else if (el.fireEvent) el.fireEvent('on' + evt.type, evt); return evt; };
eventShield.mouseEvent = function (type, sx, sy, cx, cy) { var evt; var e = { bubbles: true, cancelable: (type != "mousemove"), view: window, detail: 0, screenX: sx, screenY: sy, clientX: cx, clientY: cy, ctrlKey: false, altKey: false, shiftKey: false, metaKey: false, button: 0, relatedTarget: undefined, type: type }; if (typeof (document.createEvent) == "function") { evt = document.createEvent("MouseEvents"); evt.initMouseEvent(type, e.bubbles, e.cancelable, e.view, e.detail, e.screenX, e.screenY, e.clientX, e.clientY, e.ctrlKey, e.altKey, e.shiftKey, e.metaKey, e.button, document.body.parentNode); } else if (document.createEventObject) { evt = document.createEventObject(); for (prop in e) { evt[prop] = e[prop]; } evt.button = { 0: 1, 1: 4, 2: 2 }[evt.button] || evt.button; } return evt; };
eventShield.prototype.IsVisible = function () { if (this.shieldDIV.onmouseout) return;function viewPortHeight() { var de = document.documentElement; if (!!window.innerWidth) { return window.innerHeight; } else if (de && !isNaN(de.clientHeight)) { return de.clientHeight; } return de.offsetHeight; } function getPositionTop(e) { var o = 0; while (e) { o += e["offsetTop"]; e = e.offsetParent; } return o; } function isElementVisible(e) { var b = document.body, d = document.documentElement, pt = getPositionTop(e), pb = pt + e.offsetHeight, vt = Math.max(b.scrollTop, d.scrollTop), vb = vt + viewPortHeight(); return ((pb >= vt) && (pt <= vb)); } var v = isElementVisible(this.shieldedDIV); if (!v) { this.Activ() }; };
eventShield.prototype.Activ = function () { var th = this; $(this.shieldDIV).show(); this.shieldDIV.onmouseout = function () { th.DeactivEnd(); } };
eventShield.prototype.Deactiv = function () { var th = this; if (this.shieldTimeoutID !== null) clearTimeout(this.shieldTimeoutID); this.shieldTimeoutID = null; $(this.shieldDIV).hide(); this.shieldDIV.onmouseout = null; };
eventShield.prototype.DeactivStart = function () { this.shieldTimeoutID = setTimeout("eventShieldTAB['" + this.shieldID + "'].Deactiv()", this.ms); };
eventShield.prototype.MouseMove = function () {if (this.shieldTimeoutID !== null) clearTimeout(this.shieldTimeoutID); this.shieldTimeoutID = setTimeout("eventShieldTAB['" + this.shieldID + "'].Deactiv()", this.ms); };
eventShield.prototype.MouseClick = function (e) { if (!e) var e = window.event; this.Deactiv(); if (typeof document.elementFromPoint == 'function') { var el = document.elementFromPoint(e.clientX, e.clientY); if (el === null) return; eventShield.dispatchEvent(el, eventShield.mouseEvent("click", e.screenX, e.screenY, e.clientX, e.clientY)); } };
eventShield.prototype.DeactivEnd = function () { if (this.shieldTimeoutID !== null) { clearTimeout(this.shieldTimeoutID); this.shieldTimeoutID = null; } };

  $.fn.eventShield = function( options ) {

	var settings = $.extend( {timeout: 1000}, options );
	
	return this.each(function() {
	var $div = $( this ); 
	
	if ($div.hasClass('eventShield')) return;
	if ($div.hasClass('leaflet-container')) $div = $div.parent(); // special osm treatment - must shield the parent, not the OSM container directly
	
	var ID = $div.attr('id');		
	if (ID === void 0)
	{
	    ID = 'auto'+ eventShieldCNT;
		$div.attr('id', ID);
		eventShieldCNT++;
	};
	
	new eventShield(ID, settings.timeout);
	});
	
	return this;
};

$('.eventShield').eventShield();

});       

</script>

  window.handleCallbackOSM = function(callback) {callback();$(".leaflet-container").eventShield();};

  <script type="text/javascript">
(function(){
    "use strict";
    var params = {"before":"box-map"};
    var what = document.getElementById("stock-photo-gallery");
    var referenceId = (params.before !== void 0 ? params.before : params.after)
    var where = document.getElementById(referenceId);
    if (what !== null && where !== null)
    {
        what.parentNode.removeChild(what);
        if (params.before !== void 0)
        {
            where.parentNode.insertBefore(what, where);
        }
        else /* after */
        {
            if (where.nextSibling !== null)
                where.parentNode.insertBefore(what, where.nextSibling);
            else
                where.parentNode.appendChild(what);
        }
        if (params.style)
        {
            for(name in params.style)
            {
                if (params.style.hasOwnProperty(name))
                {
                    what.style[name] = params.style[name];
                }
            }
        }
    }
    $('img.lazy').lazyload();
}(jQuery));

$(function(){
    function run(){
            function formatItemAutocomplete(row) {
                if(typeof(row[1]) != "undefined" && row[1] !== null) {
                    return row[0] + " (<i>pop. " + row[1] + "</i>)";
                }
            }

            $("#city_left").each(function(){
                    $(this).autocomplete('/city-compare/ajax_city.php', {
                                    delay:100,
                                    minChars:3,
                                    formatItem:formatItemAutocomplete
                    }).result(function (evt, data, formatted) {
                    })
            })


            $("#city_right").each(function(){
                    $(this).autocomplete('/city-compare/ajax_city.php', {
                                    delay:100,
                                    minChars:3,
                                    formatItem:formatItemAutocomplete
                    }).result(function (evt, data, formatted) {
                    })
            })
            $(".btn-submit").click(function () {
                $("#city_form").submit();
            });

            $('#city_left').keypress(function (e) {
              if (e.which == 13) {
                $('form#city_form').submit();
                return false;
              }
            });
            $('#city_right').keypress(function (e) {
              if (e.which == 13) {
                $('form#city_form').submit();
                return false;
              }
            });

    }
    run();
});

 (function($) {
 
 function has3d() {
 
 if (window.ua.mobile) return false;
 if (!window.getComputedStyle) return false;
 

 var el = document.createElement('p'), 
 has3d,
 transforms = {
 'webkitTransform':'-webkit-transform',
 'OTransform':'-o-transform',
 'msTransform':'-ms-transform',
 'MozTransform':'-moz-transform',
 'transform':'transform'
 };
 
 // Add it to the body to get the computed style.
 document.body.insertBefore(el, null);

 for (var t in transforms) {
 if (el.style[t] !== undefined) {
 el.style[t] = "translate3d(1px,1px,1px)";
 has3d = window.getComputedStyle(el).getPropertyValue(transforms[t]);
 }
 }

 document.body.removeChild(el);

 return (has3d !== undefined && has3d.length > 0 && has3d !== "none");
 }


 function flipItInit()
 {
 $('body').off('mousemove',flipItInit);
 
 if (!has3d()) return;
 
 // if it's supported, remove the scroll effect add the cool card flipping instead
 $('.thumb.scroll').removeClass('scroll').addClass('flip');	
 //secure IE11 from flipping image during page load
 $('.thumb-detail').css("display","block");
 
 // add/remove flip class that make the transition effect
 $('.thumb.flip').hover(
 function () {$(this).find('.thumb-wrapper').addClass('flipIt');},
 function () {$(this).find('.thumb-wrapper').removeClass('flipIt');}
 );
 };
 
 $('body').on('mousemove',flipItInit);
 
 
 function loadImg(img)
 { 
 img.sizes = $(img).data("sizes");
 img.srcset = $(img).data("srcset"); 
 }	
 $('img.lazySRC').lazyload({ appear: function(){loadImg(this);}});
 
 })(jQuery); /* city/local-time.js */
 $(document).ready(function(){ if (typeof showtm === 'function') {showtm(0); setInterval('showtm(1)', 1000); }});
 /* base/responsive-graphs.js */
 (function($) {
 $("canvas,.chart,[data-highcharts-chart]").css({"max-width": "100%"});
 }(jQuery));

  <script>function play(url) {
  var f = "toolbar=no,location=no,directories=no,status=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=no,resizable=yes,copyhistory=no,width=790,height=585";
  wn = window.open("/w8/bgm"+url+".gif","_blank",f);
  if (window.focus) {
    wn.focus();
  }
}

  var f = "toolbar=no,location=no,directories=no,status=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=no,resizable=yes,copyhistory=no,width=790,height=585";
  wn = window.open("/w9/bfm"+url+".gif","_blank",f);

    wn.focus();
  }
